\documentclass[11pt]{article}

    \usepackage[breakable]{tcolorbox}
    \usepackage{parskip} % Stop auto-indenting (to mimic markdown behaviour)
    

    % Basic figure setup, for now with no caption control since it's done
    % automatically by Pandoc (which extracts ![](path) syntax from Markdown).
    \usepackage{graphicx}
    % Keep aspect ratio if custom image width or height is specified
    \setkeys{Gin}{keepaspectratio}
    % Maintain compatibility with old templates. Remove in nbconvert 6.0
    \let\Oldincludegraphics\includegraphics
    % Ensure that by default, figures have no caption (until we provide a
    % proper Figure object with a Caption API and a way to capture that
    % in the conversion process - todo).
    \usepackage{caption}
    \DeclareCaptionFormat{nocaption}{}
    \captionsetup{format=nocaption,aboveskip=0pt,belowskip=0pt}

    \usepackage{float}
    \floatplacement{figure}{H} % forces figures to be placed at the correct location
    \usepackage{xcolor} % Allow colors to be defined
    \usepackage{enumerate} % Needed for markdown enumerations to work
    \usepackage{geometry} % Used to adjust the document margins
    \usepackage{amsmath} % Equations
    \usepackage{amssymb} % Equations
    \usepackage{textcomp} % defines textquotesingle
    % Hack from http://tex.stackexchange.com/a/47451/13684:
    \AtBeginDocument{%
        \def\PYZsq{\textquotesingle}% Upright quotes in Pygmentized code
    }
    \usepackage{upquote} % Upright quotes for verbatim code
    \usepackage{eurosym} % defines \euro

    \usepackage{iftex}
    \ifPDFTeX
        \usepackage[T1]{fontenc}
        \IfFileExists{alphabeta.sty}{
              \usepackage{alphabeta}
          }{
              \usepackage[mathletters]{ucs}
              \usepackage[utf8x]{inputenc}
          }
    \else
        \usepackage{fontspec}
        \usepackage{unicode-math}
    \fi

    \usepackage{fancyvrb} % verbatim replacement that allows latex
    \usepackage{grffile} % extends the file name processing of package graphics
                         % to support a larger range
    \makeatletter % fix for old versions of grffile with XeLaTeX
    \@ifpackagelater{grffile}{2019/11/01}
    {
      % Do nothing on new versions
    }
    {
      \def\Gread@@xetex#1{%
        \IfFileExists{"\Gin@base".bb}%
        {\Gread@eps{\Gin@base.bb}}%
        {\Gread@@xetex@aux#1}%
      }
    }
    \makeatother
    \usepackage[Export]{adjustbox} % Used to constrain images to a maximum size
    \adjustboxset{max size={0.9\linewidth}{0.9\paperheight}}

    % The hyperref package gives us a pdf with properly built
    % internal navigation ('pdf bookmarks' for the table of contents,
    % internal cross-reference links, web links for URLs, etc.)
    \usepackage{hyperref}
    % The default LaTeX title has an obnoxious amount of whitespace. By default,
    % titling removes some of it. It also provides customization options.
    \usepackage{titling}
    \usepackage{longtable} % longtable support required by pandoc >1.10
    \usepackage{booktabs}  % table support for pandoc > 1.12.2
    \usepackage{array}     % table support for pandoc >= 2.11.3
    \usepackage{calc}      % table minipage width calculation for pandoc >= 2.11.1
    \usepackage[inline]{enumitem} % IRkernel/repr support (it uses the enumerate* environment)
    \usepackage[normalem]{ulem} % ulem is needed to support strikethroughs (\sout)
                                % normalem makes italics be italics, not underlines
    \usepackage{soul}      % strikethrough (\st) support for pandoc >= 3.0.0
    \usepackage{mathrsfs}
    

    
    % Colors for the hyperref package
    \definecolor{urlcolor}{rgb}{0,.145,.698}
    \definecolor{linkcolor}{rgb}{.71,0.21,0.01}
    \definecolor{citecolor}{rgb}{.12,.54,.11}

    \let\PY@ul=\relax \let\PY@tc=\relax%
    \let\PY@bc=\relax \let\PY@ff=\relax}

    \PY@it{\PY@bf{\PY@ff{#1}}}}}}}

    % For linebreaks inside Verbatim environment from package fancyvrb.
    \makeatletter
        \newbox\Wrappedcontinuationbox
        \newbox\Wrappedvisiblespacebox
        \newcommand*\Wrappedvisiblespace {\textcolor{red}{\textvisiblespace}}
        \newcommand*\Wrappedcontinuationsymbol {\textcolor{red}{\llap{\tiny$\m@th\hookrightarrow$}}}
        \newcommand*\Wrappedcontinuationindent {3ex }
        \newcommand*\Wrappedafterbreak {\kern\Wrappedcontinuationindent\copy\Wrappedcontinuationbox}
        % Take advantage of the already applied Pygments mark-up to insert
        % potential linebreaks for TeX processing.
        %        {, <, #, %, $, ' and ": go to next line.
        %        _, }, ^, &, >, - and ~: stay at end of broken line.
        % Use of \textquotesingle for straight quote.
        \newcommand*\Wrappedbreaksatspecials {%
            \def\PYGZus{\discretionary{\char`\_}{\Wrappedafterbreak}{\char`\_}}%
            \def\PYGZob{\discretionary{}{\Wrappedafterbreak\char`\{}{\char`\{}}%
            \def\PYGZcb{\discretionary{\char`\}}{\Wrappedafterbreak}{\char`\}}}%
            \def\PYGZca{\discretionary{\char`\^}{\Wrappedafterbreak}{\char`\^}}%
            \def\PYGZam{\discretionary{\char`\&}{\Wrappedafterbreak}{\char`\&}}%
            \def\PYGZlt{\discretionary{}{\Wrappedafterbreak\char`\<}{\char`\<}}%
            \def\PYGZgt{\discretionary{\char`\>}{\Wrappedafterbreak}{\char`\>}}%
            \def\PYGZsh{\discretionary{}{\Wrappedafterbreak\char`\#}{\char`\#}}%
            \def\PYGZpc{\discretionary{}{\Wrappedafterbreak\char`\%}{\char`\%}}%
            \def\PYGZdl{\discretionary{}{\Wrappedafterbreak\char`\$}{\char`\$}}%
            \def\PYGZhy{\discretionary{\char`\-}{\Wrappedafterbreak}{\char`\-}}%
            \def\PYGZsq{\discretionary{}{\Wrappedafterbreak\textquotesingle}{\textquotesingle}}%
            \def\PYGZdq{\discretionary{}{\Wrappedafterbreak\char`\"}{\char`\"}}%
            \def\PYGZti{\discretionary{\char`\~}{\Wrappedafterbreak}{\char`\~}}%
        }
        % Some characters . , ; ? ! / are not pygmentized.
        % This macro makes them "active" and they will insert potential linebreaks
        \newcommand*\Wrappedbreaksatpunct {%
            \lccode`\~`\.\lowercase{\def~}{\discretionary{\hbox{\char`\.}}{\Wrappedafterbreak}{\hbox{\char`\.}}}%
            \lccode`\~`\,\lowercase{\def~}{\discretionary{\hbox{\char`\,}}{\Wrappedafterbreak}{\hbox{\char`\,}}}%
            \lccode`\~`\;\lowercase{\def~}{\discretionary{\hbox{\char`\;}}{\Wrappedafterbreak}{\hbox{\char`\;}}}%
            \lccode`\~`\:\lowercase{\def~}{\discretionary{\hbox{\char`\:}}{\Wrappedafterbreak}{\hbox{\char`\:}}}%
            \lccode`\~`\?\lowercase{\def~}{\discretionary{\hbox{\char`\?}}{\Wrappedafterbreak}{\hbox{\char`\?}}}%
            \lccode`\~`\!\lowercase{\def~}{\discretionary{\hbox{\char`\!}}{\Wrappedafterbreak}{\hbox{\char`\!}}}%
            \lccode`\~`\/\lowercase{\def~}{\discretionary{\hbox{\char`\/}}{\Wrappedafterbreak}{\hbox{\char`\/}}}%
            \catcode`\.\active
            \catcode`\,\active
            \catcode`\;\active
            \catcode`\:\active
            \catcode`\?\active
            \catcode`\!\active
            \catcode`\/\active
            \lccode`\~`\~
        }
    \makeatother

    \let\OriginalVerbatim=\Verbatim
    \makeatletter
    \renewcommand{\Verbatim}[1][1]{%
        %\parskip\z@skip
        \sbox\Wrappedcontinuationbox {\Wrappedcontinuationsymbol}%
        \sbox\Wrappedvisiblespacebox {\FV@SetupFont\Wrappedvisiblespace}%
        \def\FancyVerbFormatLine ##1{\hsize\linewidth
            \vtop{\raggedright\hyphenpenalty\z@\exhyphenpenalty\z@
                \doublehyphendemerits\z@\finalhyphendemerits\z@
                \strut ##1\strut}%
        }%
        % If the linebreak is at a space, the latter will be displayed as visible
        % space at end of first line, and a continuation symbol starts next line.
        % Stretch/shrink are however usually zero for typewriter font.
        \def\FV@Space {%
            \nobreak\hskip\z@ plus\fontdimen3\font minus\fontdimen4\font
            \discretionary{\copy\Wrappedvisiblespacebox}{\Wrappedafterbreak}
            {\kern\fontdimen2\font}%
        }%

        % Allow breaks at special characters using \PYG... macros.
        \Wrappedbreaksatspecials
        % Breaks at punctuation characters . , ; ? ! and / need catcode=\active
        \OriginalVerbatim[#1,codes*=\Wrappedbreaksatpunct]%
    }
    \makeatother

    \definecolor{outcolor}{HTML}{D84315}
    \definecolor{cellborder}{HTML}{CFCFCF}
    \definecolor{cellbackground}{HTML}{F7F7F7}

    % prompt
    \makeatletter
    \newcommand{\boxspacing}{\kern\kvtcb@left@rule\kern\kvtcb@boxsep}
    \makeatother
    \newcommand{\prompt}[4]{
        {\ttfamily\llap{{\color{#2}[#3]:\hspace{3pt}#4}}\vspace{-\baselineskip}}
    }
    

    
    % Prevent overflowing lines due to hard-to-break entities
    \sloppy

      breaklinks=true,  % so long urls are correctly broken across lines
      colorlinks=true,
      urlcolor=urlcolor,
      linkcolor=linkcolor,
      citecolor=citecolor,
      }

\begin{document}
    
    \maketitle
    
    

    
    \section{BIA Project Pyspark}\label{bia-project-pyspark}

    \subsection{PHASE 1}\label{phase-1}

    \#Project bootstrap + load sample parquet + create label + basic splits

    1.1 Constants, paths and Spark defaults (run once per notebook)

    \begin{tcolorbox}[breakable, size=fbox, boxrule=1pt, pad at break*=1mm,colback=cellbackground, colframe=cellborder]

    1.4 Making a modeling split (month-based \& random sanity split) Because
there's no year/date, month split is ``pseudo-time''. We'll still do it

    Checks:

Schema is clean + complete for modeling: time (MONTH, DAY\_OF\_WEEK,
DEP\_TIME\_BLK), operational (CONCURRENT\_FLIGHTS, seats, plane age),
airport + carrier (DEPARTING\_AIRPORT, PREVIOUS\_AIRPORT,
CARRIER\_NAME), plus weather already merged (PRCP, SNOW, SNWD, TMAX,
AWND).

Label exists (DEP\_DEL15)

Class imbalance (delay rate):

delay=1: 122,816 delay=0: 525,501 That's \textasciitilde19\% delayed,
use class weights and report PR-AUC + Recall@TopK.

Month split sizes look reasonable for pseudo-time split.

    \section{Phase 2}\label{phase-2}

    Feature Engineering \& Leakage-safe Aggregates, additionally ``Gold''
dataset

    \begin{enumerate}
\def\labelenumi{\arabic{enumi}.}
\tightlist
\item
  Parse DEP\_TIME\_BLK → hour → cyclic sin/cos
\item
  Bucket high-cardinality categoricals (airport/carrier) to control OHE
  blow-up
\item
  Build leakage-safe historical delay rate features computed on train
  only
\item
  Assemble a final features vector and write to GCS as gold
\end{enumerate}

    Ouput Checks:

Train split: 484,002 rows with label counts 0=388,927, 1=95,075 → delay
rate ≈ 19.65\% (95,075 / 484,002).

Cyclic features (hour\_sin/cos etc.).

Top-N bucketing working (shows \textbf{OTHER} appearing).

Leakage-safe aggregates (counts + smoothed rates ).

Class weights for imbalance: w0 ≈ 0.622, w1 ≈ 2.545

    \section{Phase 3}\label{phase-3}

    ML pipeline + metrics + saved artifacts (models/preds/metrics to GCS)

    Modeling + evaluation framework:

\begin{enumerate}
\def\labelenumi{\arabic{enumi}.}
\item
  Logistic Regression (weighted)
\item
  GBTClassifier (weighted)
\item
  ROC-AUC, PR-AUC
\item
  Confusion matrix + Precision/Recall/F1 @ threshold
\item
  Recall@TopK\% (e.g., 5\%)
\item
  Cost-aware expected cost (FN cost \textgreater{} FP cost)
\item
  Brier score + calibration bins
\item
  Saving predictions + metrics + models to GCS
\end{enumerate}

    \begin{tcolorbox}[breakable, size=fbox, boxrule=1pt, pad at break*=1mm,colback=cellbackground, colframe=cellborder]
\prompt{In}{incolor}{16}{\boxspacing}
\begin{Verbatim}[commandchars=\\\{\}]

    3.3 Building Spark ML pipeline (StringIndexer → OHE → Imputer →
VectorAssembler → optional scaling)

    \begin{tcolorbox}[breakable, size=fbox, boxrule=1pt, pad at break*=1mm,colback=cellbackground, colframe=cellborder]
\prompt{In}{incolor}{ }{\boxspacing}
\begin{Verbatim}[commandchars=\\\{\}]
\PY{k+kn}{from}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{n+nn}{pyspark}\PY{n+nn}{.}\PY{n+nn}{ml}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{k+kn}{import} \PY{n}{Pipeline}
\PY{k+kn}{from}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{n+nn}{pyspark}\PY{n+nn}{.}\PY{n+nn}{ml}\PY{n+nn}{.}\PY{n+nn}{feature}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{k+kn}{import} \PY{n}{StringIndexer}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{OneHotEncoder}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{Imputer}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{VectorAssembler}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{StandardScaler}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Convert all categoricals to string (esp ints like DISTANCE\PYZus{}GROUP)}
\PY{k}{for} \PY{n}{c} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{n}{cat\PYZus{}cols}\PY{p}{:}
    \PY{n}{train} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{train}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{withColumn}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{c}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{F}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{col}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{c}\PY{p}{)}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{cast}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{string}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{n}{val}   \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{val}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{withColumn}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{c}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{F}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{col}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{c}\PY{p}{)}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{cast}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{string}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{n}{test}  \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{test}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{withColumn}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{c}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{F}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{col}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{c}\PY{p}{)}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{cast}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{string}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}

\PY{n}{indexers} \PY{o}{=} \PY{p}{[}
    \PY{n}{StringIndexer}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{inputCol}\PY{o}{=}\PY{n}{c}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{outputCol}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+s+sa}{f}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{c}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZus{}idx}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{handleInvalid}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{keep}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{k}{for} \PY{n}{c} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{n}{cat\PYZus{}cols}
\PY{p}{]}

\PY{n}{encoder} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{OneHotEncoder}\PY{p}{(}
    \PY{n}{inputCols}\PY{o}{=}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+sa}{f}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{c}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZus{}idx}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}} \PY{k}{for} \PY{n}{c} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{n}{cat\PYZus{}cols}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{,}
    \PY{n}{outputCols}\PY{o}{=}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+sa}{f}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{c}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZus{}ohe}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}} \PY{k}{for} \PY{n}{c} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{n}{cat\PYZus{}cols}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{,}
    \PY{n}{handleInvalid}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{keep}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}
\PY{p}{)}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Impute numeric nulls using TRAIN statistics}
\PY{n}{imputer} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{Imputer}\PY{p}{(}
    \PY{n}{inputCols}\PY{o}{=}\PY{n}{num\PYZus{}cols}\PY{p}{,}
    \PY{n}{outputCols}\PY{o}{=}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+sa}{f}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{c}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZus{}imp}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}} \PY{k}{for} \PY{n}{c} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{n}{num\PYZus{}cols}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{,}
    \PY{n}{strategy}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{median}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}
\PY{p}{)}

\PY{n}{assembled\PYZus{}inputs} \PY{o}{=} \PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+sa}{f}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{c}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZus{}imp}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}} \PY{k}{for} \PY{n}{c} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{n}{num\PYZus{}cols}\PY{p}{]} \PY{o}{+} \PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+sa}{f}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{c}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZus{}ohe}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}} \PY{k}{for} \PY{n}{c} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{n}{cat\PYZus{}cols}\PY{p}{]}

\PY{n}{assembler} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{VectorAssembler}\PY{p}{(}
    \PY{n}{inputCols}\PY{o}{=}\PY{n}{assembled\PYZus{}inputs}\PY{p}{,}
    \PY{n}{outputCol}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{features\PYZus{}raw}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{,}
    \PY{n}{handleInvalid}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{keep}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}
\PY{p}{)}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Optional but recommended for Logistic Regression}
\PY{n}{scaler} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{StandardScaler}\PY{p}{(}
    \PY{n}{inputCol}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{features\PYZus{}raw}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{,}
    \PY{n}{outputCol}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{features}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{,}
    \PY{n}{withMean}\PY{o}{=}\PY{k+kc}{False}\PY{p}{,}   \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} keep False for sparse}
    \PY{n}{withStd}\PY{o}{=}\PY{k+kc}{True}
\PY{p}{)}

\PY{n}{feature\PYZus{}pipeline} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{Pipeline}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{stages}\PY{o}{=}\PY{n}{indexers} \PY{o}{+} \PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{encoder}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{imputer}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{assembler}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{scaler}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n}{feat\PYZus{}model} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{feature\PYZus{}pipeline}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{fit}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{train}\PY{p}{)}

\PY{n}{train\PYZus{}fe} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{feat\PYZus{}model}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{transform}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{train}\PY{p}{)}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{select}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{label}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{,}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{weight}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{,}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{features}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}

    Cache feature datasets once (prevents repeated recomputation)

    Spark WARN warnings: sending a large serialized ``task'' to executors

The pipeline/model object being shipped is big (OHE metadata, many
stages), running transformations inside Python helper functions and
Spark ends up serializing more than expected.

Fix:

    \begin{tcolorbox}[breakable, size=fbox, boxrule=1pt, pad at break*=1mm,colback=cellbackground, colframe=cellborder]

    3.6 Evaluation on VAL, picking threshold, then evaluating TEST

(We'll pick a threshold that maximizes F1 on validation (can also pick
cost-minimizing).

    \begin{tcolorbox}[breakable, size=fbox, boxrule=1pt, pad at break*=1mm,colback=cellbackground, colframe=cellborder]
\prompt{In}{incolor}{34}{\boxspacing}
\begin{Verbatim}[commandchars=\\\{\}]
\PY{k}{def}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{n+nf}{eval\PYZus{}model}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{name}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{model}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{df\PYZus{}fe}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
    \PY{n}{pred} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{model}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{transform}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{df\PYZus{}fe}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{n}{pred} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{add\PYZus{}prob}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{pred}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{n}{roc}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{pr} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{basic\PYZus{}auc\PYZus{}metrics}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{pred}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{k}{return} \PY{n}{pred}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{roc}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{pr}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} \PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{} Validation \PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}}
\PY{n}{lr\PYZus{}val\PYZus{}pred}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{lr\PYZus{}val\PYZus{}roc}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{lr\PYZus{}val\PYZus{}pr} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{eval\PYZus{}model}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{lr}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{lr\PYZus{}model}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{val\PYZus{}fe}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n}{gbt\PYZus{}val\PYZus{}pred}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{gbt\PYZus{}val\PYZus{}roc}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{gbt\PYZus{}val\PYZus{}pr} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{eval\PYZus{}model}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{gbt}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{gbt\PYZus{}model}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{val\PYZus{}fe}\PY{p}{)}

\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{LR  VAL  ROC\PYZhy{}AUC:}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{lr\PYZus{}val\PYZus{}roc}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{PR\PYZhy{}AUC:}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{lr\PYZus{}val\PYZus{}pr}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{GBT VAL  ROC\PYZhy{}AUC:}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{gbt\PYZus{}val\PYZus{}roc}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{PR\PYZhy{}AUC:}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{gbt\PYZus{}val\PYZus{}pr}\PY{p}{)}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Threshold sweep on validation}
\PY{n}{thresholds} \PY{o}{=} \PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{i}\PY{o}{/}\PY{l+m+mi}{100} \PY{k}{for} \PY{n}{i} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{n+nb}{range}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mi}{10}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mi}{91}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mi}{5}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{]}

\PY{k}{def}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{n+nf}{best\PYZus{}thr}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{df\PYZus{}prob}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
    \PY{n}{stats} \PY{o}{=} \PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{confusion\PYZus{}metrics}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{df\PYZus{}prob}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{t}\PY{p}{)} \PY{k}{for} \PY{n}{t} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{n}{thresholds}\PY{p}{]}
    \PY{n}{best} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n+nb}{max}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{stats}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{key}\PY{o}{=}\PY{k}{lambda} \PY{n}{d}\PY{p}{:} \PY{n}{d}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{f1}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{k}{return} \PY{n}{best}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{stats}

\PY{n}{lr\PYZus{}best}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{\PYZus{}}  \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{best\PYZus{}thr}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{lr\PYZus{}val\PYZus{}pred}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n}{gbt\PYZus{}best}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{\PYZus{}} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{best\PYZus{}thr}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{gbt\PYZus{}val\PYZus{}pred}\PY{p}{)}

\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{LR best thr:}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{lr\PYZus{}best}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{GBT best thr:}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{gbt\PYZus{}best}\PY{p}{)}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Extra val metrics}
\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{LR recall@top5}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZpc{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{:}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{recall\PYZus{}at\PYZus{}topk\PYZus{}fast}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{lr\PYZus{}val\PYZus{}pred}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mf}{0.05}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}

    \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} pick best threshold by F1 on validation}
    \PY{n}{stats} \PY{o}{=} \PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{confusion\PYZus{}metrics}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{val\PYZus{}pred}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{t}\PY{p}{)} \PY{k}{for} \PY{n}{t} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{n}{thresholds}\PY{p}{]}
    \PY{n}{best} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n+nb}{max}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{stats}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{key}\PY{o}{=}\PY{k}{lambda} \PY{n}{d}\PY{p}{:} \PY{n}{d}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{f1}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{n}{best} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{add\PYZus{}accuracy\PYZus{}to\PYZus{}conf}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{best}\PY{p}{)}

    \PY{n}{val\PYZus{}top5} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{recall\PYZus{}at\PYZus{}topk\PYZus{}fast}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{val\PYZus{}pred}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mf}{0.05}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{recall\PYZus{}at\PYZus{}topk}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{]}

\PY{k+kn}{from}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{n+nn}{pyspark}\PY{n+nn}{.}\PY{n+nn}{sql}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{k+kn}{import} \PY{n}{functions} \PY{k}{as} \PY{n}{F}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Get list of metric columns (everything except \PYZsq{}model\PYZsq{})}
\PY{n}{metric\PYZus{}cols} \PY{o}{=} \PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{c} \PY{k}{for} \PY{n}{c} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{n}{summary\PYZus{}df}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{columns} \PY{k}{if} \PY{n}{c} \PY{o}{!=} \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{model}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{]}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Round all metric columns to 4 decimal places inside Spark}
\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} This keeps it as a Spark DataFrame}
\PY{n}{rounded\PYZus{}df} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{summary\PYZus{}df}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{select}\PY{p}{(}
    \PY{n}{F}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{col}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{model}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{,}
    \PY{o}{*}\PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{F}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{round}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{F}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{col}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{c}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mi}{4}\PY{p}{)}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{alias}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{c}\PY{p}{)} \PY{k}{for} \PY{n}{c} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{n}{metric\PYZus{}cols}\PY{p}{]}
\PY{p}{)}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Create the \PYZdq{}Stack\PYZdq{} expression dynamically}
\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} This converts wide format to long format: | model | metric\PYZus{}name | value |}
\PY{n}{stack\PYZus{}string} \PY{o}{=} \PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{, }\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{join}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+sa}{f}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{c}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{, }\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{c}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}} \PY{k}{for} \PY{n}{c} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{n}{metric\PYZus{}cols}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n}{stack\PYZus{}expr} \PY{o}{=} \PY{l+s+sa}{f}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{stack(}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n+nb}{len}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{metric\PYZus{}cols}\PY{p}{)}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{, }\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{stack\PYZus{}string}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{) as (metric, value)}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Transform: Stack \PYZhy{}\PYZgt{} GroupBy \PYZhy{}\PYZgt{} Pivot}
\PY{n}{transposed\PYZus{}df} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{rounded\PYZus{}df}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{select}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{model}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{F}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{expr}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{stack\PYZus{}expr}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)} \PYZbs{}
    \PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{groupBy}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{metric}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)} \PYZbs{}
    \PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{pivot}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{model}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)} \PYZbs{}
    \PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{agg}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{F}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{first}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{value}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)} \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} taking first value since there\PYZsq{}s 1 value per model/metric}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Display in native PySpark }
\PY{n}{transposed\PYZus{}df}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{show}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{n}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+m+mi}{100}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{truncate}\PY{o}{=}\PY{k+kc}{False}\PY{p}{)}
\end{Verbatim}
\end{tcolorbox}

    \section{Phase 4}\label{phase-4}

    Ablation study (Base → +Congestion → +Weather → Full)

Creating four feature sets. The current ``Full'' is already:

\begin{enumerate}
\def\labelenumi{\arabic{enumi}.}
\item
  Base: time + simple flight attributes (no congestion/weather)
\item
  +Congestion: add CONCURRENT\_FLIGHTS + monthly traffic features
\item
  +Weather: add weather fields
\item
  Full: base + congestion + weather + leakage-safe aggregates
\end{enumerate}

    Defining feature groups

    \begin{tcolorbox}[breakable, size=fbox, boxrule=1pt, pad at break*=1mm,colback=cellbackground, colframe=cellborder]
\prompt{In}{incolor}{43}{\boxspacing}

    Helper to build features for a given set

    \begin{tcolorbox}[breakable, size=fbox, boxrule=1pt, pad at break*=1mm,colback=cellbackground, colframe=cellborder]
\prompt{In}{incolor}{44}{\boxspacing}
\begin{Verbatim}[commandchars=\\\{\}]
\PY{k+kn}{from}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{n+nn}{pyspark}\PY{n+nn}{.}\PY{n+nn}{ml}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{k+kn}{import} \PY{n}{Pipeline}
\PY{k+kn}{from}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{n+nn}{pyspark}\PY{n+nn}{.}\PY{n+nn}{ml}\PY{n+nn}{.}\PY{n+nn}{feature}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{k+kn}{import} \PY{n}{StringIndexer}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{OneHotEncoder}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{Imputer}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{VectorAssembler}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{StandardScaler}

\PY{k}{def}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{n+nf}{build\PYZus{}feature\PYZus{}pipeline}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{cat\PYZus{}cols}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{num\PYZus{}cols}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
    \PY{n}{indexers} \PY{o}{=} \PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{StringIndexer}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{inputCol}\PY{o}{=}\PY{n}{c}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{outputCol}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+s+sa}{f}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{c}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZus{}idx}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{handleInvalid}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{keep}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)} \PY{k}{for} \PY{n}{c} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{n}{cat\PYZus{}cols}\PY{p}{]}
    \PY{n}{encoder} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{OneHotEncoder}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{inputCols}\PY{o}{=}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+sa}{f}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{c}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZus{}idx}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}} \PY{k}{for} \PY{n}{c} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{n}{cat\PYZus{}cols}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{,}
                            \PY{n}{outputCols}\PY{o}{=}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+sa}{f}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{c}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZus{}ohe}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}} \PY{k}{for} \PY{n}{c} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{n}{cat\PYZus{}cols}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{,}
                            \PY{n}{handleInvalid}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{keep}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{n}{imputer} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{Imputer}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{inputCols}\PY{o}{=}\PY{n}{num\PYZus{}cols}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{outputCols}\PY{o}{=}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+sa}{f}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{c}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZus{}imp}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}} \PY{k}{for} \PY{n}{c} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{n}{num\PYZus{}cols}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{strategy}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{median}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{n}{assembler} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{VectorAssembler}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{inputCols}\PY{o}{=}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+sa}{f}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{c}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZus{}imp}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}} \PY{k}{for} \PY{n}{c} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{n}{num\PYZus{}cols}\PY{p}{]} \PY{o}{+} \PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+sa}{f}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{c}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZus{}ohe}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}} \PY{k}{for} \PY{n}{c} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{n}{cat\PYZus{}cols}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{,}
                                \PY{n}{outputCol}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{features\PYZus{}raw}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{handleInvalid}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{keep}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{n}{scaler} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{StandardScaler}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{inputCol}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{features\PYZus{}raw}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{outputCol}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{features}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{withMean}\PY{o}{=}\PY{k+kc}{False}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{withStd}\PY{o}{=}\PY{k+kc}{True}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{k}{return} \PY{n}{Pipeline}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{stages}\PY{o}{=}\PY{n}{indexers} \PY{o}{+} \PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{encoder}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{imputer}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{assembler}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{scaler}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{)}
\end{Verbatim}

    Train + evaluate ablation models fast (only trains 4 models)

    \begin{tcolorbox}[breakable, size=fbox, boxrule=1pt, pad at break*=1mm,colback=cellbackground, colframe=cellborder]
\prompt{In}{incolor}{48}{\boxspacing}
\begin{Verbatim}[commandchars=\\\{\}]
\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} from pyspark.ml.feature import VectorAssembler}
\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} from pyspark.ml.classification import GBTClassifier}
\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} from pyspark.sql import Row}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} def make\PYZus{}feats(df\PYZus{}full, input\PYZus{}cols, out\PYZus{}col):}
\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{}     \PYZsh{} drop out\PYZus{}col if it already exists to avoid collisions}
\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{}     df = df\PYZus{}full.drop(out\PYZus{}col) if out\PYZus{}col in df\PYZus{}full.columns else df\PYZus{}full}
\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{}     return VectorAssembler(inputCols=input\PYZus{}cols, outputCol=out\PYZus{}col, handleInvalid=\PYZdq{}keep\PYZdq{}).transform(df)}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} def run\PYZus{}ablation\PYZus{}fast(name, input\PYZus{}cols):}
\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{}     out\PYZus{}col = \PYZdq{}features\PYZus{}abl\PYZdq{}}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{}     tr = make\PYZus{}feats(full\PYZus{}tr, input\PYZus{}cols, out\PYZus{}col).select(\PYZdq{}label\PYZdq{},\PYZdq{}weight\PYZdq{},F.col(out\PYZus{}col).alias(\PYZdq{}features\PYZdq{})).cache(); \PYZus{} = tr.count()}
\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{}     va = make\PYZus{}feats(full\PYZus{}va, input\PYZus{}cols, out\PYZus{}col).select(\PYZdq{}label\PYZdq{},\PYZdq{}weight\PYZdq{},F.col(out\PYZus{}col).alias(\PYZdq{}features\PYZdq{})).cache(); \PYZus{} = va.count()}
\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{}     te = make\PYZus{}feats(full\PYZus{}te, input\PYZus{}cols, out\PYZus{}col).select(\PYZdq{}label\PYZdq{},\PYZdq{}weight\PYZdq{},F.col(out\PYZus{}col).alias(\PYZdq{}features\PYZdq{})).cache(); \PYZus{} = te.count()}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{}     model = GBTClassifier(featuresCol=\PYZdq{}features\PYZdq{}, labelCol=\PYZdq{}label\PYZdq{}, weightCol=\PYZdq{}weight\PYZdq{},}
\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{}                           maxIter=40, maxDepth=4, stepSize=0.08, subsamplingRate=0.8).fit(tr)}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{}     summary, \PYZus{}, \PYZus{} = evaluate\PYZus{}classifier(name, model, va, te, thresholds=[i/100 for i in range(10, 91, 5)])}
\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{}     return Row(**summary)}
\end{Verbatim}
\end{tcolorbox}

    Changed ablation assembler output to a new column name, like
features\_abl, and then training GBT on that.

\begin{enumerate}
\def\labelenumi{\arabic{enumi}.}
\item
  builds features\_abl
\item
  renames it to features only in the small training/val/test DFs passed
  to the classifier
\item
  avoids any collision with your original features column
\end{enumerate}

    Code to prevent a few giant partitions from slowing down each ablation
run.

    \begin{Verbatim}[commandchars=\\\{\}]
Saved ablation to: gs://big-data-
project-481305-flightdelay/airline/metrics/ablation\_study/
    \end{Verbatim}

    Why it's slow (current ablation)

Each run\_ablation\_fast() does:

\begin{enumerate}
\def\labelenumi{\arabic{enumi}.}
\item
  assemble features + cache + count() (3 full actions per ablation)
\item
  train a GBT (heavy)
\item
  evaluate\_classifier() does:
\end{enumerate}

\begin{itemize}
\tightlist
\item
  transform val/test
\item
  AUC calculations
\item
  threshold sweep (many passes)
\item
  Recall@TopK (often involves sorting)
\end{itemize}

    \section{Slice metrics by airport / time block /
month}\label{slice-metrics-by-airport-time-block-month}

We'll compute per-slice counts, delay rate, avg predicted risk, and
optionally precision/recall at the chosen threshold.

    Example using best model predictions (using GBT test preds):

    \section{Why slicing matters for the
project}\label{why-slicing-matters-for-the-project}

\begin{enumerate}
\def\labelenumi{\arabic{enumi}.}
\item
  Operational usefulness Airlines don't act on ``overall PR-AUC.'' They
  act by airport, time block, carrier, month. Slicing tells you where
  the model predicts high risk so operations can allocate
  buffers/crew/gates.
\item
  Diagnose hidden failure modes

  ** A model can look strong overall but fail badly at:
\end{enumerate}

\begin{itemize}
\tightlist
\item
  specific airports (hub congestion patterns)
\item
  early morning vs evening banks
\item
  winter months vs summer Slicing surfaces those weak spots.
\end{itemize}

\begin{enumerate}
\def\labelenumi{\arabic{enumi}.}
\setcounter{enumi}{2}
\item
  Model reliability / generalization

  If your avg\_pred\_risk tracks delay\_rate by slice, that's evidence
  your model is learning real structure, not noise.
\item
  Mini drift check

  If monthly delay\_rate shifts but your avg\_pred\_risk doesn't, that's
  drift/miscalibration.

  Even without full production monitoring, this is a solid ``big data
  ML'' deliverable.
\item
  Supports that feature engineering is important

  can show that adding weather/congestion improved hardest slices
  (winter months, busy time blocks, specific airports).
\end{enumerate}

    \begin{tcolorbox}[breakable, size=fbox, boxrule=1pt, pad at break*=1mm,colback=cellbackground, colframe=cellborder]
\prompt{In}{incolor}{53}{\boxspacing}
\begin{Verbatim}[commandchars=\\\{\}]
\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Choose which model preds you want to slice (example: GBT)}
\PY{n}{thr} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{gbt\PYZus{}summary}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{best\PYZus{}thr}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{]}   \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} if your variable is different, change here}
\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} thr = gbt\PYZus{}best[\PYZdq{}thr\PYZdq{}]         \PYZsh{} if that\PYZsq{}s what you used earlier}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Build predictions WITH row\PYZus{}id}
\PY{n}{gbt\PYZus{}test\PYZus{}pred} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{add\PYZus{}prob}\PY{p}{(}
    \PY{n}{gbt\PYZus{}model}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{transform}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{test\PYZus{}fe}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{select}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{row\PYZus{}id}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{,}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{label}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{,}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{weight}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{,}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{features}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{p}{)}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{select}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{row\PYZus{}id}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{,}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{label}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{,}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{p1}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{cache}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}

    \PY{n}{test\PYZus{}fe}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{select}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{row\PYZus{}id}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{,}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{MONTH}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{,}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{DEP\PYZus{}TIME\PYZus{}BLK}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{,}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{DEPARTING\PYZus{}AIRPORT\PYZus{}BKT}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{,}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{CARRIER\PYZus{}NAME\PYZus{}BKT}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{,}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{label}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{join}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{gbt\PYZus{}test\PYZus{}pred}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{select}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{row\PYZus{}id}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{,}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{p1}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{on}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{row\PYZus{}id}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{how}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{inner}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{withColumn}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{pred}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{F}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{col}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{p1}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)} \PY{o}{\PYZgt{}}\PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{F}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{lit}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{thr}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{cast}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{int}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{p}{)}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{cache}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}

    \begin{Verbatim}[commandchars=\\\{\}]

    \begin{Verbatim}[commandchars=\\\{\}]
Saved slice outputs to: gs://big-data-
project-481305-flightdelay/airline/metrics/slices/20251221\_035129/
    \end{Verbatim}

    Below is a simple way to explain \textbf{exactly what outputs are
saying},

\begin{center}\rule{0.5\linewidth}{0.5pt}\end{center}

\section{1) Airport slice
(DEPARTING\_AIRPORT\_BKT)}\label{airport-slice-departing_airport_bkt}

\textbf{How to read it:} For each airport, compare:

\begin{itemize}
\tightlist
\item
  \textbf{delay\_rate} = actual \% delayed
\item
  \textbf{avg\_pred\_risk} = model's average predicted probability
\item
  \textbf{pred\_positive\_rate} = \% flagged as ``delay'' at your
  threshold
\end{itemize}

\section{What table shows}\label{what-table-shows}

\begin{itemize}
\item
  The model assigns \textbf{high predicted risk
  (\textasciitilde0.35--0.48)} to many airports, but the \textbf{actual
  delay\_rate is much lower (\textasciitilde0.11--0.25)} for most of
  them. → This means the model is \textbf{systematically pessimistic}
  (over-predicting delay probabilities).
\item
  The biggest example is \textbf{Chicago O'Hare (ORD)}:
  \textbf{delay\_rate ≈ 0.160}, \textbf{avg\_pred\_risk ≈ 0.449},
  \textbf{pred\_positive\_rate ≈ 0.332} → It flags \textasciitilde33\%
  as delays while only \textasciitilde16\% are truly delayed (lots of
  false positives).
\item
  Airports like \textbf{JFK}: \textbf{delay\_rate ≈ 0.154},
  \textbf{avg\_pred\_risk ≈ 0.426}, \textbf{pred\_positive\_rate ≈
  0.318} → Again, flagged rate is about \textbf{2×} the true delay rate.
\end{itemize}

\textbf{Simple takeaway:} The model is ranking airports (some look
riskier than others), but overall it's \textbf{over-flagging delays}
across airports.

\begin{center}\rule{0.5\linewidth}{0.5pt}\end{center}

\section{2) Time-block slice
(DEP\_TIME\_BLK)}\label{time-block-slice-dep_time_blk}

\section{What table shows}\label{what-table-shows-1}

\begin{itemize}
\item
  Early morning has \textbf{lower delay\_rate} and the model also
  outputs \textbf{lower avg\_pred\_risk}:

  \begin{itemize}
  \tightlist
  \item
    \textbf{0600--0659:} delay\_rate ≈ 0.071, avg\_pred\_risk ≈ 0.203
  \item
    \textbf{0700--0759:} delay\_rate ≈ 0.084, avg\_pred\_risk ≈ 0.246
  \end{itemize}
\item
  Late afternoon/evening has \textbf{higher delay\_rate} and the model
  predicts higher risk:

  \begin{itemize}
  \tightlist
  \item
    \textbf{1800--1859:} delay\_rate ≈ 0.222, avg\_pred\_risk ≈ 0.522,
    pred\_positive\_rate ≈ 0.560
  \item
    \textbf{1900--1959:} delay\_rate ≈ 0.233, avg\_pred\_risk ≈ 0.527,
    pred\_positive\_rate ≈ 0.582
  \end{itemize}
\end{itemize}

\textbf{Simple takeaway:} This is a strong ``makes sense'' result:
delays \textbf{accumulate through the day}, and the model reflects that.
But it still flags \textbf{way too many} late-day flights as delayed
(pred\_positive\_rate \textasciitilde0.56 vs true \textasciitilde0.22).

\begin{center}\rule{0.5\linewidth}{0.5pt}\end{center}

\section{3) Month slice (MONTH)}\label{month-slice-month}

only have \textbf{months 11 and 12} here (so your test set seems to be
Nov/Dec).

\begin{itemize}
\tightlist
\item
  \textbf{Month 12:} delay\_rate ≈ 0.193, avg\_pred\_risk ≈ 0.399,
  pred\_positive\_rate ≈ 0.273
\item
  \textbf{Month 11:} delay\_rate ≈ 0.131, avg\_pred\_risk ≈ 0.384,
  pred\_positive\_rate ≈ 0.243
\end{itemize}

\textbf{Simple takeaway:} December is truly worse than November (higher
delay\_rate), and your model also predicts higher risk in December.
Again, predicted probabilities are roughly \textbf{2×} the actual delay
rate.

\begin{center}\rule{0.5\linewidth}{0.5pt}\end{center}

\section{4) Carrier slice
(CARRIER\_NAME\_BKT)}\label{carrier-slice-carrier_name_bkt}

\section{What table shows}\label{what-table-shows-2}

\begin{itemize}
\item
  Some carriers have clearly higher delay rates:

  \begin{itemize}
  \tightlist
  \item
    \textbf{JetBlue:} delay\_rate ≈ 0.233, avg\_pred\_risk ≈ 0.494,
    pred\_positive\_rate ≈ 0.487
  \item
    \textbf{Frontier:} delay\_rate ≈ 0.236, avg\_pred\_risk ≈ 0.499,
    pred\_positive\_rate ≈ 0.541
  \item
    \textbf{Southwest:} delay\_rate ≈ 0.203, avg\_pred\_risk ≈ 0.409,
    pred\_positive\_rate ≈ 0.371
  \end{itemize}
\item
  Others are much lower:

  \begin{itemize}
  \tightlist
  \item
    \textbf{Hawaiian:} delay\_rate ≈ 0.067, avg\_pred\_risk ≈ 0.235,
    pred\_positive\_rate ≈ 0.051 → Here the model is much more
    reasonable and flags fewer delays.
  \end{itemize}
\end{itemize}

\textbf{Simple takeaway:} The model captures carrier-level differences
(some carriers do have higher delay rates). For many carriers it still
predicts too aggressively (predicted risk and flag-rate too high).

\begin{center}\rule{0.5\linewidth}{0.5pt}\end{center}

\section{Conlcusion}\label{conlcusion}

``Slicing shows the model captures real operational patterns (later time
blocks, December, and certain carriers/airports are riskier), but it is
generally over-predicting delay probability and flagging too many
flights as delayed---suggesting the threshold and/or calibration should
be adjusted.''

    \begin{tcolorbox}[breakable, size=fbox, boxrule=1pt, pad at break*=1mm,colback=cellbackground, colframe=cellborder]
\prompt{In}{incolor}{ }{\boxspacing}
\begin{Verbatim}[commandchars=\\\{\}]

\end{Verbatim}
\end{tcolorbox}

    \section{KMeans clustering: PCA visualization + profiling +
intra-distance
table}\label{kmeans-clustering-pca-visualization-profiling-intra-distance-table}

    Rebuild a numeric features vector from available columns:

\begin{itemize}
\tightlist
\item
  compute cluster centers from data
\item
  compute intra\_cluster\_distance
\item
  PCA for visualization
\item
  profiling table
\end{itemize}

              \PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{groupBy}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{CLUSTER\PYZus{}COL}\PY{p}{)}
              \PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{agg}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{F}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{sort\PYZus{}array}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{F}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{collect\PYZus{}list}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{F}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{struct}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{pos}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{,}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{mean\PYZus{}val}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{alias}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{tmp}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}
              \PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{withColumn}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{center\PYZus{}arr}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{F}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{transform}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{tmp}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{k}{lambda} \PY{n}{s}\PY{p}{:} \PY{n}{s}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{mean\PYZus{}val}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}
              \PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{drop}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{tmp}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} 4) Join centers back + intra\PYZhy{}cluster distance}
\PY{n}{df2} \PY{o}{=} \PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{df\PYZus{}arr}

    \subsection{Cluster Narratives (KMeans + PCA +
Profiling)}\label{cluster-narratives-kmeans-pca-profiling}

\subsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Cluster 0 --- ``Typical baseline
flights''
\emph{(n=158,889)}}{Cluster 0 --- ``Typical baseline flights'' (n=158,889)}}\label{cluster-0-typical-baseline-flights-n158889}

\begin{itemize}
\tightlist
\item
  Mid-level congestion (\textbf{26.95}), typical aircraft size
  (\textbf{\textasciitilde124.7 seats}) and older fleet
  (\textbf{\textasciitilde12.3 yrs}).
\item
  Mild weather overall (\textbf{PRCP 0.099}, tiny snow), moderate temp
  (\textbf{TMAX 57.8}) and wind (\textbf{AWND 8.69}).
\item
  Mid-year timing (\textbf{Month \textasciitilde6}) and mid-distance
  routes (\textbf{Dist group 3.13}).
\end{itemize}

\subsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Cluster 1 --- ``Hot \& dry operations''
\emph{(n=167,149)}}{Cluster 1 --- ``Hot \& dry operations'' (n=167,149)}}\label{cluster-1-hot-dry-operations-n167149}

\begin{itemize}
\tightlist
\item
  More congested (\textbf{28.73}) with typical aircraft
  (\textbf{\textasciitilde125.8 seats}) and older fleet
  (\textbf{\textasciitilde12.36 yrs}).
\item
  Completely snow-free (\textbf{SNOW 0}, \textbf{SNWD 0}) and hottest
  conditions (\textbf{TMAX 85.6}) with moderate wind (\textbf{7.74}).
\item
  Skews later in the year (\textbf{Month \textasciitilde7.26}).
\end{itemize}

\subsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Cluster 2 --- ``Winter storm / disruption
regime''
\emph{(n=39,704)}}{Cluster 2 --- ``Winter storm / disruption regime'' (n=39,704)}}\label{cluster-2-winter-storm-disruption-regime-n39704}

\begin{itemize}
\tightlist
\item
  Smallest but most variable cluster (\textbf{avg intra-dist 5.10}).
\item
  Strongest weather severity: highest precip (\textbf{0.218}), heavy
  snow (\textbf{0.478}) and snow depth (\textbf{1.392}), coldest temps
  (\textbf{TMAX 38.5}) and highest wind (\textbf{11.48}).
\item
  Earlier-year timing (\textbf{Month \textasciitilde4.92}). This is the
  \textbf{high-risk conditions} regime that separates clearly in PCA.
\end{itemize}

\subsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Cluster 3 --- ``Warm, low-snow, shorter
routes''
\emph{(n=172,490)}}{Cluster 3 --- ``Warm, low-snow, shorter routes'' (n=172,490)}}\label{cluster-3-warm-low-snow-shorter-routes-n172490}

\begin{itemize}
\tightlist
\item
  Highest congestion (\textbf{29.07}) with typical seats
  (\textbf{\textasciitilde122.4}) and older planes
  (\textbf{\textasciitilde12.51 yrs}).
\item
  Near-zero snow, warm temps (\textbf{TMAX 77.1}), lower precip
  (\textbf{0.085}).
\item
  Slightly shorter routes (\textbf{Dist group 2.84}) and mid-to-late
  year timing (\textbf{Month \textasciitilde6.89}).
\end{itemize}

\subsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Cluster 4 --- ``Long-haul / large
aircraft / newer fleet''
\emph{(n=110,085)}}{Cluster 4 --- ``Long-haul / large aircraft / newer fleet'' (n=110,085)}}\label{cluster-4-long-haul-large-aircraft-newer-fleet-n110085}

\begin{itemize}
\tightlist
\item
  Lower congestion (\textbf{26.00}) but much larger planes
  (\textbf{\textasciitilde180.8 seats}) and newer fleet
  (\textbf{\textasciitilde7.62 yrs}).
\item
  Low precip and minimal snow, warm temps (\textbf{TMAX 72.9}).
\item
  Very long routes (\textbf{Dist group 7.60}). This is the distinct
  \textbf{big-plane long-haul} segment.
\end{itemize}

    Cluster compactness ranking (best/worst clusters)

    \begin{tcolorbox}[breakable, size=fbox, boxrule=1pt, pad at break*=1mm,colback=cellbackground, colframe=cellborder]

\begin{Verbatim}[commandchars=\\\{\}]
\PY{n}{cluster\PYZus{}quality} \PY{o}{=} \PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{df2}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{groupBy}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{CLUSTER\PYZus{}COL}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{agg}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{F}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{count}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{*}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{alias}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{n}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{,}
         \PY{n}{F}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{avg}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{intra\PYZus{}cluster\PYZus{}distance}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{alias}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{avg\PYZus{}dist}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{,}
         \PY{n}{F}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{expr}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{percentile\PYZus{}approx(intra\PYZus{}cluster\PYZus{}distance, 0.5)}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{alias}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{median\PYZus{}dist}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{,}
         \PY{n}{F}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{expr}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{percentile\PYZus{}approx(intra\PYZus{}cluster\PYZus{}distance, 0.9)}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{alias}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{p90\PYZus{}dist}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{orderBy}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{F}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{desc}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{avg\PYZus{}dist}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}

\PY{n}{cluster\PYZus{}quality}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{show}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mi}{50}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{truncate}\PY{o}{=}\PY{k+kc}{False}\PY{p}{)}

    Explaining the clusters from profiling output

    Based on table:

\begin{itemize}
\item
  Cluster 2:

  Highest intra distance (\textasciitilde5.10) → most ``mixed'' cluster
  Highest PRCP (0.218) + highest SNOW (0.478) + highest SNWD (1.392)
  Lowest TMAX (38.46) + highest AWND (11.48)
\end{itemize}

Interpretation: ``Severe winter weather / windy conditions cluster (high
variability).''

\begin{itemize}
\item
  Cluster 1:

  Lowest intra distance (2.41) → most compact cluster PRCP (0.112), SNOW
  = 0, SNWD = 0, TMAX high (85.62)
\end{itemize}

Interpretation: ``Clear-weather warm-season cluster (stable
operations).''

\begin{itemize}
\item
  Cluster 4:

  Very high seat count (180.84) + lowest plane age (7.62) distance group
  much larger (7.60)
\end{itemize}

Interpretation: ``Longer-haul / larger aircraft segment (structurally
different fleet/route).''

\begin{itemize}
\item
  Cluster 0 \& 3:

  Similar planes/temps but different snow/temps (cluster 3 shows higher
  snow; cluster 0 moderate).
\end{itemize}

Interpretation: ``Normal operations clusters split by seasonal
temperature/precip regime.''

    

    \begin{center}\rule{0.5\linewidth}{0.5pt}\end{center}

\section{Analysis of Cluster Visualization (PCA
Projection)**}\label{analysis-of-cluster-visualization-pca-projection}

The 2D Principal Component Analysis (PCA) projection reveals three
distinct operational patterns within the flight data:

\textbf{1. The High-Risk Weather Regime (Cluster 2 -- Green)}
*Observation:** Cluster 2 is strictly isolated, stretching far to the
right along Principal Component 1 (PC1). Its center (marked by `X') is
clearly separated from the rest of the data points.

\begin{itemize}
\tightlist
\item
  *Interpretation:\textbf{ This represents a rare but statistically
  significant }''Operational Regime''** that deviates sharply from
  typical flights. Correlating this with the feature profiling, this
  cluster is defined by:

  \begin{itemize}
  \tightlist
  \item
    Much higher \texttt{PRCP}, \texttt{SNOW}, and \texttt{SNWD}
  \item
    Higher Wind Speeds
  \item
    Lower \texttt{TMAX}
  \item
    \emph{Summary:} A severe winter weather / disruption regime.
  \end{itemize}
\end{itemize}

\begin{quote}
\textbf{Project Meaning:} The clustering algorithm is successfully
isolating the \textbf{high-risk weather regime}. This is a critical
validation for the project, confirming that the model can distinguish
``disruption days'' from standard operations without supervision.
\end{quote}

\begin{center}\rule{0.5\linewidth}{0.5pt}\end{center}

\textbf{2. Normal Operations \& Structural Overlap (Clusters 0, 1, 3)}
*Observation:** Clusters 0, 1, and 3 overlap heavily near the origin
(approx. \(PC1 \in [-1, 1]\) and \(PC2 \in [-2, 2]\)).

\begin{itemize}
\tightlist
\item
  *Interpretation:\textbf{ These groups represent }''Normal
  Operations''** where differences are subtler. While K-Means separates
  them based on the full high-dimensional feature space, they appear
  mixed in 2D because PCA only displays the top two directions of
  variance.
\end{itemize}

\begin{quote}
\textbf{Project Meaning:} The visual overlap is \textbf{not a failure};
it is a known limitation of 2D PCA projections. These clusters likely
represent valid segments based on fleet, route, or time patterns that do
not manifest as extreme outliers in the top two principal components.
\end{quote}

\begin{center}\rule{0.5\linewidth}{0.5pt}\end{center}

\textbf{3. The Long-Haul / Large Fleet Segment (Cluster 4 -- Purple)}
*Observation:** Cluster 4 is distinct due to its vertical separation,
sitting significantly higher on the PC2 axis.

\begin{itemize}
\tightlist
\item
  *Interpretation:\textbf{ This vertical shift indicates a difference in
  }structural patterns** rather than weather severity. Based on feature
  profiling, Cluster 4 is characterized by:

  \begin{itemize}
  \tightlist
  \item
    Very high \texttt{NUMBER\_OF\_SEATS}
  \item
    Lower \texttt{PLANE\_AGE}
  \item
    Much larger \texttt{DISTANCE\_GROUP}
  \item
    \emph{Summary:} A segment for larger aircraft and long-haul
    operations.
  \end{itemize}
\end{itemize}

\begin{quote}
\textbf{Project Meaning:} This identifies a valuable business segment.
\textbf{Long-haul and large-aircraft operations} behave differently
logistically, implying their delay risk patterns will differ from
regional flights. Segregating this group allows the model to learn these
specific nuances.
\end{quote}

\begin{center}\rule{0.5\linewidth}{0.5pt}\end{center}

    

    \section{Project Impact: Why Clustering
Matters}\label{project-impact-why-clustering-matters}

\begin{itemize}
\item
  Uncovers Operational Regimes Moves beyond ``black-box'' prediction by
  proving distinct flight categories exist (e.g., Severe Weather
  vs.~Long-Haul), validating the data structure.
\item
  Boosts Model Performance The Cluster\_ID acts as a powerful
  ``meta-feature'' that summarizes complex conditions. Adding it to the
  classifier improves key metrics like PR-AUC and Recall.
\item
  Diagnoses Model Errors Provides context for failures. Mispredictions
  within the ``Severe Weather'' cluster can be attributed to inherent
  environmental volatility rather than model insufficiency.
\end{itemize}

\end{Verbatim}
\end{tcolorbox}

    7.3 Spike scoring (robust z-score) + visuals (Matplotlib)

Core anomaly logic:

\begin{itemize}
\tightlist
\item
  Compare each segment's delay rate to its own baseline
\item
  Use robust z-score (median/MAD) so outliers don't break the detector
\item
  Flag ``spikes'' as abs(z) \textgreater= 3.5
\end{itemize}

    \begin{tcolorbox}[breakable, size=fbox, boxrule=1pt, pad at break*=1mm,colback=cellbackground, colframe=cellborder]
\prompt{In}{incolor}{66}{\boxspacing}
\begin{Verbatim}[commandchars=\\\{\}]
\PY{k+kn}{import}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{n+nn}{numpy}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{k}{as}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{n+nn}{np}
\PY{k+kn}{import}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{n+nn}{pandas}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{k}{as}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{n+nn}{pd}
\PY{k+kn}{import}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{n+nn}{matplotlib}\PY{n+nn}{.}\PY{n+nn}{pyplot}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{k}{as}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{n+nn}{plt}

\PY{k}{def}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{n+nf}{robust\PYZus{}z}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{series}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
\PY{+w}{    }\PY{l+s+sd}{\PYZdq{}\PYZdq{}\PYZdq{}Robust z\PYZhy{}score using median + MAD.\PYZdq{}\PYZdq{}\PYZdq{}}
    \PY{n}{s} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{np}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{asarray}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{series}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{dtype}\PY{o}{=}\PY{n+nb}{float}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{n}{med} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{np}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{median}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{s}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{n}{mad} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{np}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{median}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{np}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{abs}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{s} \PY{o}{\PYZhy{}} \PY{n}{med}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)} \PY{o}{+} \PY{l+m+mf}{1e\PYZhy{}9}
    \PY{n}{z} \PY{o}{=} \PY{l+m+mf}{0.6745} \PY{o}{*} \PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{s} \PY{o}{\PYZhy{}} \PY{n}{med}\PY{p}{)} \PY{o}{/} \PY{n}{mad}
    \PY{k}{return} \PY{n}{z}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{med}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{mad}

\PY{n}{Z\PYZus{}THR} \PY{o}{=} \PY{l+m+mf}{3.0}   \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} robust spike threshold (3.5 is common)}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} \PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}}
\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} A) Monthly drift/spike plots}
\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} \PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}}
\PY{n}{pdf\PYZus{}m} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{monthly}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{toPandas}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{sort\PYZus{}values}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{MONTH}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Robust z + stats for delay rate}
\PY{n}{z\PYZus{}delay}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{med\PYZus{}delay}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{mad\PYZus{}delay} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{robust\PYZus{}z}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{pdf\PYZus{}m}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{delay\PYZus{}rate}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{]}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{values}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n}{pdf\PYZus{}m}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{z\PYZus{}delay}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{]} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{z\PYZus{}delay}
\PY{n}{pdf\PYZus{}m}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{anomaly\PYZus{}delay}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{]} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{np}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{abs}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{pdf\PYZus{}m}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{z\PYZus{}delay}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{)} \PY{o}{\PYZgt{}}\PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{Z\PYZus{}THR}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Robust z + stats for avg predicted risk}
\PY{n}{z\PYZus{}risk}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{med\PYZus{}risk}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{mad\PYZus{}risk} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{robust\PYZus{}z}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{pdf\PYZus{}m}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{avg\PYZus{}pred\PYZus{}risk}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{]}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{values}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n}{pdf\PYZus{}m}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{z\PYZus{}risk}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{]} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{z\PYZus{}risk}
\PY{n}{pdf\PYZus{}m}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{anomaly\PYZus{}risk}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{]} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{np}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{abs}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{pdf\PYZus{}m}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{z\PYZus{}risk}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{)} \PY{o}{\PYZgt{}}\PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{Z\PYZus{}THR}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Convert Z\PYZus{}THR into value\PYZhy{}threshold bands for easy plotting:}
\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} z = 0.6745*(x\PYZhy{}med)/mad  =\PYZgt{}  x = med + (z*mad)/0.6745}
\PY{k}{def}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{n+nf}{z\PYZus{}to\PYZus{}value\PYZus{}band}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{med}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{mad}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{zthr}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
    \PY{n}{delta} \PY{o}{=} \PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{zthr} \PY{o}{*} \PY{n}{mad}\PY{p}{)} \PY{o}{/} \PY{l+m+mf}{0.6745}
    \PY{k}{return} \PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{med} \PY{o}{\PYZhy{}} \PY{n}{delta}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{med} \PY{o}{+} \PY{n}{delta}\PY{p}{)}

\PY{n}{delay\PYZus{}lo}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{delay\PYZus{}hi} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{z\PYZus{}to\PYZus{}value\PYZus{}band}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{med\PYZus{}delay}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{mad\PYZus{}delay}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{Z\PYZus{}THR}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n}{risk\PYZus{}lo}\PY{p}{,}  \PY{n}{risk\PYZus{}hi}  \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{z\PYZus{}to\PYZus{}value\PYZus{}band}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{med\PYZus{}risk}\PY{p}{,}  \PY{n}{mad\PYZus{}risk}\PY{p}{,}  \PY{n}{Z\PYZus{}THR}\PY{p}{)}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} \PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{} Plot 1: Monthly Delay Rate \PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}}

    \begin{Verbatim}[commandchars=\\\{\}]
Spike months (delay\_rate): []
Spike months (avg\_pred\_risk): []
    \end{Verbatim}

    \begin{verbatim}
Monthly charts:
\end{verbatim}

\begin{itemize}
\item
  These plots show how the actual delay rate and the model's average
  predicted delay risk change month-by-month, making seasonal spikes
  easy to spot.
\item
  Months where both rise together indicate true operational stress
  periods (weather/traffic), not just model noise.
\end{itemize}

    \begin{verbatim}
Month × Time Block heatmap:
\end{verbatim}

\begin{itemize}
\item
  This heatmap pinpoints when during the day delays concentrate within
  each month, highlighting recurring ``hot'' time windows (often late
  afternoon/evening).
\item
  The ``top spike cells'' list is your anomaly report: the most
  unusually high delay pockets by month and time block.
\end{itemize}

    \section{Where did the spikes come from?'' (airport/carrier
drivers)}\label{where-did-the-spikes-come-from-airportcarrier-drivers}

This produces a bar chart of the most anomalous airports (per-month vs
that airport's normal).

    \begin{tcolorbox}[breakable, size=fbox, boxrule=1pt, pad at break*=1mm,colback=cellbackground, colframe=cellborder]

    \section{Scale-IN experiment (10\% → 25\% → 50\% →
100\%)}\label{scale-in-experiment-10-25-50-100}

    Scaling Strategy: Progressive `Scale-In'

We adopted a progressive `Scale-In' strategy to efficiently validate
pipeline integrity and optimize hyperparameters. By incrementally
increasing data volume, we ensure model stability and resource
efficiency before committing to full-scale training.

20\% (\textasciitilde2M): Validate schema, pipeline, and baselines

50\% (\textasciitilde5M): Hyperparameter tuning (TrainValidationSplit)

75\% (\textasciitilde7.5M): Stability \& calibration check across
time/segments

100\% (\textasciitilde10M): Final training + full evaluation

    \begin{tcolorbox}[breakable, size=fbox, boxrule=1pt, pad at break*=1mm,colback=cellbackground, colframe=cellborder]
\prompt{In}{incolor}{71}{\boxspacing}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} \PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}}
\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} 3) Run scale\PYZhy{}up grid}
\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} \PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}}
